### [315] [Automated High-Precision Extraction and Forensic Verification of Data-Bearing Vector Figures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31345)
*Bowen Sun,Chaowei Xiao*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套从矢量科学图表中自动恢复精确数值数据的方法，包括精度理论、自动提取器和验证机制，能够实现比特级精确恢复（matplotlib标记可达float32精度），并通过重渲染证书确保结果不可否认。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学文献中的数值数据越来越多地以图表形式呈现，而非文本或表格。读者若需获取底层数值，通常只能手动重新数字化，过程缓慢、不精确且无法证明结果的忠实性。

Method: 三部分贡献：(1) 精度理论，界定给定渲染器和导出格式下数据恢复的理论精度边界；(2) 自动提取器，无需人工干预，一次遍历即可解码图表；(3) 验证理论，证明恢复是单射的，偶然冲突概率极低，并通过重渲染证书实现不可否认性。

Result: 无需真实数据参与恢复，解码结果与外部档案高度吻合：Planck 2018数据精度达10^-9，Keeling CO2记录达5×10^-4；独立恢复的图表可复现Chinchilla缩放律置信区间的修正结果。

Conclusion: 该方法能够提供经过认证的可信数据恢复，但恢复出的数值需要人工审查，而非作为指控依据。任何具体数据集的科学意义不在本文讨论范围内。

Abstract: The quantitative record of science and engineering is increasingly carried by figures rather than text or tables, and a reader who needs the underlying numbers must usually re-digitize them by hand: slowly, imprecisely, and with no way to prove the result is faithful. Yet when a figure is stored as vector graphics, its data are not approximated by the picture but encoded in it: the renderer writes each marker and vertex at a printed precision that, for the dominant scientific toolchain, exceeds the data's own. We turn this into three contributions, one per shortcoming of hand digitization. First, a precision theory bounding how accurately data can be recovered for a given renderer and export format: bit-exact float32 for matplotlib markers, and a calibration-limited three to four significant figures end to end. Second, an automatic extractor that decodes a figure in one pass with no human in the loop, in place of the slow point-by-point tracing a digitizer demands. Third, a verification theory: recovery is injective except on a characterized, vanishingly small interval near zero; accidental agreement between unrelated data is astronomically unlikely; and a re-rendering certificate binds the recovered values to the markers, lines, and ticks the figure draws, not its text, making a result non-repudiable. With no ground truth used during recovery, decoded figures match external archives (Planck 2018 to 10^-9; the Keeling CO2 record to 5*10^-4, and one decoded figure independently reproduces a correction to the Chinchilla scaling-law confidence interval. We map the achievable precision across common renderers and their PDF, SVG, and EPS formats. What we deliver is certified data; the scientific significance of any particular dataset lies outside this paper's scope, and recovered values are candidates for human review, never accusations.

</details>


### [316] [Witness Complexity of Short Descriptions: A Cryptographic Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31370)
*Fabio F. G. Buono*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出"见证复杂度" \(\gam(x)\)，衡量字符串在通用图灵机上最短描述的最小运行时间，填补了紧凑表示与可验证性之间的形式化鸿沟。该度量不同于熵和Kolmogorov复杂度，证明其与P vs NP问题的关联，并应用于密钥和证书的可用性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密码学实践中，短密钥或证书必须在有界时间内可扩展或可验证才有实际可用性；而现有度量（如Kolmogorov复杂度）仅关注描述长度，忽略了解压缩或验证所需的时间成本。因此需要一种同时衡量描述长度与计算时间的复杂度度量。

Method: 定义见证复杂度 \(\gam(x)\) 为字符串在通用图灵机上"近乎最短"描述的最小运行时间；证明其多项式因子的不变性；利用P≠NP假设给出条件分离；利用KC的不可计算性给出无条件下界；给出与P=NP等价的二条件刻画；对结构化NP族证明多项式时间可处理性。第二部分发展了配套度量并展示了文法大小与派生代价之间的无条件鸿沟。

Result: \(\gam\) 与Shannon熵和Kolmogorov复杂度不同，低KC可以与高\(\gam\)共存；证明了多项式因子下的不变性；条件分离（假设P≠NP）；来自KC不可计算性的无条件下界；与P=NP等价的二条件刻画；对结构化NP族的多项式时间可处理性；以及文法大小与派生代价之间的无条件鸿沟。

Conclusion: 见证复杂度 \(\gam\) 作为密钥和证书可用性的度量，弥补了紧凑表示与有界时间验证之间的形式化鸿沟，为密码学实践中的资源约束分析提供了新工具。

Abstract: In cryptographic practice, where protocols impose strict time bounds, implementations demand predictable resource usage, and real-world systems require immediate verification for security and usability, a short key or certificate is useful only if it can be expanded or verified within a bounded time; otherwise a compact representation that requires superpolynomial work to expand offers no operational guarantee within a bounded-time protocol. This paper formalises that gap by introducing \emph{witness complexity} \(\gam(x)\), the minimum running time over near-shortest descriptions of a string on a universal Turing machine. \(\gam\) differs from Shannon entropy and Kolmogorov complexity \(\KC\): low \(\KC\) can coexist with high \(\gam\). We prove invariance up to polynomial factors; a conditional separation (assuming \(\PneqNP\)). An unconditional lower bound from incomputability of \(\KC\); a biconditional characterisation of \(\PeqNP\) via the class-relative variant \(\gP\); and polynomial-time tractability for structured \(\classNP\) families. Part II develops companion measures and shows an unconditional gap between grammar size and derivation cost, positioning \(\gam\) as a metric for the usability of keys and certificates.

</details>

More recently, NVIDIA has developed GPU TEEs (e.g., H100/H200), yet comprehensive evaluations of end-to-end workflows that integrate CPU and GPU TEEs remain limited. ### [319] [CVE-TTP KG: Knowledge Graph Linking Software Vulnerabilities to Attack Behaviors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31557)
*Basant Agarwal,Dincy R. Arikkat,Swati Yadav,Serena Nicolazzo,Antonino Nocera,Vinod P*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文通过构建CVE-TTP知识图谱，将CVE漏洞与MITRE ATT&CK框架中的攻击者行为（战术和技术）关联起来。使用基于Transformer的模型（CySecBERT）实现行为识别（技术F1=87.71%，战术F1=96.16%），并创建了包含24,820个实体和43,608个关系的标注数据集，最终集成到Neo4j图数据库中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CVE和NVD等漏洞数据库虽然提供了详细的技术信息，但缺乏与攻击者行为（如战术和技术）的关联，导致对威胁的有效解读和响应受限。本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 构建CVE-TTP知识图谱：使用基于Transformer的模型（CySecBERT）进行行为识别；创建标注数据集（24,820实体，43,608关系）用于实体和关系抽取；采用pipeline方法（实体抽取F1=0.86，关系抽取F1=0.99）和span-based联合模型（F1=0.78）；最终集成到Neo4j图数据库中。

Result: CySecBERT在技术识别上达到87.71%的宏F1分数，在战术识别上达到96.16%；pipeline方法实体抽取F1=0.86，关系抽取F1=0.99；span-based联合模型F1=0.78。

Conclusion: 成功构建了连接漏洞与攻击者行为的知识图谱，实现了结构化的漏洞可视化，有效增强了威胁解读和响应能力。

Abstract: In the evolving threat landscape, adversaries exploit software vulnerabilities to launch sophisticated attacks, challenging traditional defenses. Although databases like CVE and NVD provide detailed technical information, they often lack links to attacker behaviors such as tactics and techniques, limiting effective threat interpretation and response. This work bridges this gap by connecting vulnerabilities with behavioral patterns from the MITRE ATT&CK framework. We construct a CVE-TTP Knowledge Graph that links CVEs to tactics and techniques using classification and relation extraction. Transformer-based models are developed for behavior identification, with CySecBERT achieving macro F1-scores of 87.71% (techniques) and 96.16% (tactics). Also, we created an annotated dataset with 24,820 entities and 43,608 relations for entity and relation extraction. The pipeline-based approach achieves macro F1-scores of 0.86 (entity extraction) and 0.99 (relation extraction), while a span-based joint model achieves 0.78. These outputs are integrated into a Neo4j-based Cyber Threat Knowledge Graph, enabling structured visualization of vulnerabilities.

</details>

### [321] [Digital signature schemes based on code equivalence and syndrome decoding from restricted errors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31601)
*Sarah Arpin,Jason T. LeGrow,Hiram H. López,Gretchen L. Matthews*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文综述了NIST后量子密码标准化进程中两种基于纠错码的候选数字签名方案（CROSS和LESS），阐述了其底层困难问题（受限错误综合征解码和码等价问题）、Sigma协议与Fiat-Shamir变换，以及如何实现抗量子安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 后量子时代需要能够抵御量子计算机攻击的数字签名方案，代码基签名是重要方向之一。

Method: 基于纠错码的困难问题（受限错误综合征解码和码等价问题），通过Sigma协议和Fiat-Shamir变换构造签名方案。

Result: 描述了CROSS和LESS两种方案的结构与安全性原理。

Conclusion: 基于纠错码的数字签名方案被认为具备后量子安全性，是抗量子签名的重要候选。

Abstract: Digital signature schemes are an important cryptographic tool to ensure data authenticity and integrity in many applications that must be resilient to attacks, including those facilitated by quantum computers. We consider the two digital signature schemes based on error-correcting codes that are second-round candidates in NIST's call for Additional Signature Schemes, which is part of the Post-Quantum Cryptography Standardization Process. Specifically, we provide an overview of the Codes and Restricted Objects Signature Scheme (CROSS) and the Linear Equivalence Signature Scheme (LESS). We describe their underlying problems of syndrome decoding from restricted errors and code equivalence. We review sigma protocols and how they can be transformed into digital signature schemes via the Fiat-Shamir transform. Finally, we explain how this procedure yields code-based digital signatures believed to be post-quantum secure.

### [322] [Hybrid Topological Data Analysis and LSTM Networks for Enhanced Network Intrusion Detection Using CIC-IDS2017 Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31619)
*Amar Jeet,Bhaskar Ranjan Karn,Dinesh Kumar*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出了一种结合拓扑数据分析(TDA)和LSTM网络的混合方法用于网络入侵检测，在CIC-IDS2017数据集上达到了近乎完美的检测性能(AUC=1.000, F1=1.000)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 网络入侵检测系统(NIDS)需要更先进的技术来检测网络流量中的恶意活动，以增强网络安全防御能力。

Method: 采用混合方法，将TDA的持续同调（Betti曲线和持久性图）与LSTM网络相结合，构建多层架构，同时捕获网络流量模式的拓扑特征和时间序列特征。

Result: 在CIC-IDS2017数据集上，混合TDA+LSTM模型达到AUC=1.000和F1=1.000；5折交叉验证平均AUC=1.000±0.000，平均F1=0.999±0.001；消融实验显示拓扑特征F1=0.990，时序特征F1=1.000；优于TDA+随机森林(F1=0.994)和孤立森林(F1=0.835)基线。

Conclusion: TDA的拓扑特征与LSTM的时序特征具有互补性，混合方法能显著提升网络入侵检测性能，在多种攻击类别上均优于传统基线方法。

Abstract: Network intrusion detection systems (NIDS) are crucial in cybersecurity infrastructure, needing advanced techniques to detect hostile activity in network traffic. This research introduces a hybrid approach that combines Topological Data Analysis (TDA) with Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) networks to improve anomaly detection in network security. Our multi-layered design combines TDA's persistent homology with LSTM networks to capture topological characteristics of network traffic patterns and simulate temporal sequences. We assessed our methodology using the CIC-IDS2017 dataset, which includes over 2.8 million labelled flows, 77 network variables, and 14 attack categories that reflect modern threat landscapes such as DDoS, brute force, web attacks, penetration, and botnet activities. Integrating Betti curves and persistence diagrams with deep learning architectures enhances feature extraction performance. Our hybrid TDA+LSTM model has an AUC of 1.000 and F1-score of 1.000, with 5-fold cross-validation producing a mean AUC of 1.000 $\pm$ 0.000 and mean F1 of 0.999 $\pm$ 0.001. An ablation research demonstrates the complimentary contributions of topological (F1=0.990) and temporal characteristics (F1=1.000). Comparative research shows that the suggested strategy beats TDA+Random Forest (F1=0.994) and Isolation Forest (F1=0.835) baselines in several attack categories.

</details>


### [323] [A Lifecycle and Application-Stack Survey of Large Language Model Vulnerabilities: Attacks, Risks, Defenses, and Open Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31639)
*Seyed Bagher Hashemi Natanzi,Bo Tang*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文通过生命周期和应用栈视角，系统梳理了大语言模型系统在数据收集、预训练、后训练对齐、模型打包与供应链、检索与记忆、提示与推理、工具/智能体执行、部署与维护等八个阶段的攻击面、防御措施及安全目标，并提出了未来研究议程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型已从单纯的文本生成器演变为嵌入检索管道、企业助手、机器人系统、自主智能体等复杂应用栈的组件，其安全风险不再仅限于模型权重本身，而是涉及数据、提示、模型输出、工具、记忆和用户权限交互的完整生命周期。现有研究缺乏系统化的安全视角，需要从生命周期和应用栈的角度整合攻击与防御知识。

Method: 采用生命周期和应用栈视角，将攻击组织为八个阶段：数据收集、预训练、后训练对齐、模型打包与供应链、检索与记忆、提示与推理、工具/智能体执行、部署与维护。对每个阶段分析攻击者能力、受影响的安全目标、代表性攻击、实际风险、评估实践和防御措施。将LLM特定漏洞映射到机密性、完整性、可用性、安全性、隐私、公平性、问责制和智能体控制等安全目标。

Result: 建立了系统化的LLM系统安全分类体系，重点揭示了信任边界的失效点、不可信数据如何变为可执行指令、委托授权如何放大模型错误，以及单点防御难以组合形成整体防护的原因。

Conclusion: 提出了面向安全LLM系统的研究议程，包括组合安全、可溯源检索、工具调用隔离、长周期智能体评估、隐私保护适配、真实场景红队测试以及部署级事件响应。

Abstract: Large language models are no longer only text generators. They are increasingly embedded in retrieval pipelines, enterprise assistants, coding environments, robotic systems, security-operation workflows, and autonomous agents that can read private data, call tools, write files, execute code, and act across organizational boundaries. This shift changes the security problem: risks do not arise from the model weights alone, but from the full lifecycle and application stack through which data, prompts, model outputs, tools, memories, and user authority interact. This paper systematizes the literature on vulnerabilities in large language model systems through a lifecycle and application-stack lens. We organize attacks across eight stages: data collection, pretraining, post-training alignment, model packaging and supply chain, retrieval and memory, prompting and inference, tool/agent execution, and deployment/maintenance. For each stage, we analyze attacker capabilities, affected security objectives, representative attacks, practical risks, evaluation practices, and defenses. We further map LLM-specific vulnerabilities to confidentiality, integrity, availability, safety, privacy, fairness, accountability, and agency-control objectives. Unlike taxonomies that list isolated attack names, the proposed systematization emphasizes where trust boundaries fail, how untrusted data becomes executable instruction, how delegated authority amplifies model errors, and why point defenses rarely compose. We close with a research agenda for secure LLM systems, including compositional security, provenance-aware retrieval, tool-call containment, long-horizon agent evaluation, privacy-preserving adaptation, realistic red teaming, and deployment-grade incident response.

</details>


### [324] [Exploring Side-Channel Protections in Hardware Implementations of PQC ML-KEM Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31681)
*Davis Ranney,Yashaswini I Makaram,A. Adam Ding,Yunsi Fei*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文研究ML-KEM在FPGA上的侧信道安全漏洞，发现FPGA并行架构导致高阶掩码设计仍存在一阶泄漏，可被用于恢复完整密钥。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ML-KEM作为后量子密码标准，其FUjisaki-Okamoto验证步骤对侧信道攻击（功耗和电磁分析）特别敏感，需要评估不同硬件平台上的安全性。

Method: 对比分析三种验证实现（未保护、基于哈希的一阶掩码、高阶掩码）在微控制器和FPGA上的侧信道泄漏，重点关注FPGA并行处理带来的影响。

Result: FPGA上的高阶掩码设计仍然存在足够的一阶泄漏，可以用于完整秘密密钥恢复。

Conclusion: 在性能受限和并行化硬件环境中，保护后量子密码算法仍然面临持久挑战。

Abstract: As ML-KEM is adopted as a post-quantum cryptographic standard, resilience against physical side-channel attacks has become essential. Among the constituent steps, the decapsulation Fujisaki-Okamoto (FO) verification is particularly vulnerable to side-channel power and electromagnetic (EM) analysis. In this work, we focus on common FPGA-based implementations and examine their side-channel vulnerabilities, and compare them with those of microcontroller implementations. Three verification implementations, unprotected, hash-based (first-order), and higher-order masked, are evaluated for side-channel security on both a microcontroller and an FPGA. While FPGAs offer higher speed and parallelism, they often exhibit stronger side-channel leakage, especially in high bandwidth configurations. The higher-order masked designs still leak information about the underlying data due to hardware-level effects and data-dependent processing. Our experiments show that their parallelized processing on FPGAs introduces sufficient first-order leakage for full secret-key recovery. These results underscore the persistent challenge of securing PQC algorithms in performance-constrained and parallelized hardware environments.

</details>


### [325] [Robocalls: A Worldwide or US-only Problem? Analyzing Spam and Fraud in International Phone Calls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31790)
*Kemal Altwlkany,Andro Merćep,Tomislav Đuričić,Ante Kapetanović,Emanuel Lacic*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 该研究通过收集来自65个国家的数据，首次公开了多模态的国际骚扰电话数据集（870万条通话记录、839份转录文本、677段录音），分析发现美国面临的骚扰电话威胁显著高于其他国家。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 骚扰电话（robocalls）造成巨大经济损失（仅2025年美国就损失11亿美元），且由于跨国法律管辖权、数据隐私、多语言等限制，国际骚扰电话研究严重不足，缺乏公开数据集。

Method: 历时9个月从65个国家收集骚扰电话数据，构建包含通话记录、转录文本和录音的多模态数据集；通过聚类分析识别28个骚扰电话活动集群，并进行跨国家对比分析。

Result: 揭示了通话模式、联合目标攻击行为、常见活动集群、回拨号码提取、同语言不同地区的语言差异等；发现美国面临的骚扰电话威胁严重程度显著高于其他国家。

Conclusion: 骚扰电话是国际性问题，但美国受害最为严重；基于分析结果提出了未来研究方向和建议对策。

Abstract: Unsolicited automated phone calls (robocalls) are a serious threat: in the US alone, these calls resulted in reported losses of 1.1$ billion during 2025. Phishing and spoofing consistently rank among the most reported crimes within the FBI's Internet Crime Complaint Center, with phone call scams having the highest reported median loss. Combating robocalls is difficult due to many legal and practical constraints: robocalls often encompass multiple legal jurisdictions of different countries/states, the large volume of robocalls, their multilingual nature, the lack of publicly available data, privacy concerns with obtaining data, etc. We present a study of international robocalls, aggregating robocall reports from countries across all inhabited continents and contribute by providing new findings on international robocalls from 65 different countries. We also present the first publicly available multimodal and international robocall dataset: 8.7 million call detail records, 839 robocall transcripts from 28 identified robocall campaign clusters, and 677 robocall recordings. We describe our methodology for collecting robocall data over a 9-month period and provide a detailed analysis comparing robocalls in the US with those in other countries. Our analysis covers several aspects, including uncovering calling patterns, identifying co-targeting attacks, discovering common robocall campaigns, extracting callback numbers, analyzing linguistic differences among robocalls in the same language but different regions, and other insights. Our results indicate that although robocalls are an international problem, the severity of the threat is significantly higher in the US than in other countries. We provide steps for future research and suggest remedies to reduce the effectiveness of robocalls based on our analysis.

</details>
